# <span data-ttu-id="5b558-104">Informações sobre a versão JavaScript</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b558-104">JavaScript Version Information</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="5b558-105">O suporte a JavaScript varia de acordo com o Microsoft Edge, os aplicativos da Microsoft Store e os diferentes modos de documento do Internet Explorer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b558-105">JavaScript support varies across Microsoft Edge, Microsoft Store apps, and different document modes of Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b558-106">Para obter mais informações sobre o controle de versão do código de documento do IE, consulte [*definindo a compatibilidade do documento*](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=208537).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b558-106">For more information about IE document code versioning, see [*Defining Document Compatibility*](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=208537).</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="5b558-107">A tabela a seguir resume o suporte a JavaScript nos aplicativos Internet Explorer, Microsoft Edge e Microsoft Store.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b558-107">The following table summarizes the JavaScript support across Internet Explorer, Microsoft Edge, and Microsoft Store apps.</span></span>  
  
> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="5b558-108">Os recursos experimentais \ (habilitados em *about: flags*\) são indicados por "exp".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b558-108">Experimental features \(enabled from *about:flags*\) are indicated by "Exp."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5b558-109">Em alguns casos, o suporte a *repositório de aplicativos* varia entre os aplicativos do Windows 8 \ (V8 \) e do Windows 10 \ (V10 \) e a área de trabalho do Windows \ (Win \) e o Windows Phone \ (telefone \), conforme indicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5b558-109">In some cases, *Store apps* support varies between Windows 8 \(v8\) and Windows 10 \(v10\) apps, and Windows desktop \(Win\) and Windows Phone \(Phone\), as indicated.</span></span>
